# ██╗     ██╗███████╗████████╗     ██████╗ ███████╗███╗   ██╗███████╗██████╗  █████╗ ██╗
# ██║     ██║██╔════╝╚══██╔══╝    ██╔════╝ ██╔════╝████╗  ██║██╔════╝██╔══██╗██╔══██╗██║
# ██║     ██║███████╗   ██║       ██║  ███╗█████╗  ██╔██╗ ██║█████╗  ██████╔╝███████║██║
# ██║     ██║╚════██║   ██║       ██║   ██║██╔══╝  ██║╚██╗██║██╔══╝  ██╔══██╗██╔══██║██║
# ███████╗██║███████║   ██║       ╚██████╔╝███████╗██║ ╚████║███████╗██║  ██║██║  ██║███████╗
# ╚══════╝╚═╝╚══════╝   ╚═╝        ╚═════╝ ╚══════╝╚═╝  ╚═══╝╚══════╝╚═╝  ╚═╝╚═╝  ╚═╝╚══════╝

gdp_grow_variable_list = {
    every_country = {
        limit = {
            has_modifier = has_central_bank
            NOT = {
                is_subject = yes

                is_subject_type = subject_type_protectorate
            }
        }
        root = {
            add_to_variable_list = {
                name = gdp_grow_variable_list
                target = prev
            }
        }
    }
    root  = {
        if = {
            clear_variable_list = list_before_order
            every_in_list = {
                variable = gdp_grow_variable_list
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = list_before_order
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
            }
            clear_variable_list = gdp_grow_variable_list_ordered_1
            if = {
                ordered_in_list = {
                    variable = list_before_order
                    order_by = GDP_dif_1_final
                    max = 15
                    check_range_bounds = no
                    root = {
                        add_to_variable_list = {
                            name = gdp_grow_variable_list_ordered_1
                            target = prev
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        clear_variable_list = gdp_grow_variable_list
    }
}
exports_imports_variable_list = {
    every_country = {
        limit = {
            has_modifier = has_central_bank
            NOT = {
                is_subject = yes

                is_subject_type = subject_type_protectorate
            }
			export_value_in_currency > 0
			import_value_in_currency > 0
        }
        root = {
            add_to_variable_list = {
                name = exports_imports_variable_list
                target = prev
            }
        }
    }
    root  = {
        if = {
            clear_variable_list = list_before_order
            every_in_list = {
                variable = exports_imports_variable_list
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = list_before_order
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
            }
            clear_variable_list = exports_imports_variable_list_ordered_1
            if = {
                ordered_in_list = {
                    variable = list_before_order
                    order_by = trade_balance_in_gold
                    max = 15
                    check_range_bounds = no
                    root = {
                        add_to_variable_list = {
                            name = exports_imports_variable_list_ordered_1
                            target = prev
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        clear_variable_list = exports_imports_variable_list
    }
}
independent_economies_list = {
    every_country = {
        limit = {
            has_modifier = has_central_bank
			has_technology_researched = gold_standard
            NOT = {
                OR = {
                    is_subject = yes

                    is_subject_type = subject_type_protectorate
                    has_law = law_type:law_isolationism
                    is_revolutionary = yes
                }
            }
        }
        root = {
            add_to_variable_list = {
                name = independent_economies_list
                target = prev
            }
        }
    }
    root  = {
        if = {
            clear_variable_list = list_before_order
            every_in_list = {
                variable = independent_economies_list
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = list_before_order
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
            }
            clear_variable_list = independent_economies_list_ordered_1
            if = {
                ordered_in_list = {
                    variable = list_before_order
                    order_by = money_value_rapported_inflation
                    max = 100
                    check_range_bounds = no
                    root = {
                        add_to_variable_list = {
                            name = independent_economies_list_ordered_1
                            target = prev
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        clear_variable_list = independent_economies_list
    }
}
dependent_economies_list = {
    every_country = {
        limit = {
            has_modifier = has_central_bank
			has_technology_researched = gold_standard
            AND = {
                or = {
                    is_subject = yes

                    is_subject_type = subject_type_protectorate
                }
            }
            NOT = {
                has_law = law_type:law_isolationism
                is_revolutionary = yes
            }
        }
        root = {
            add_to_variable_list = {
                name = dependent_economies_list
                target = prev
            }
        }
    }
    root  = {
        if = {
            clear_variable_list = list_before_order
            every_in_list = {
                variable = dependent_economies_list
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = list_before_order
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
            }
            clear_variable_list = dependent_economies_list_ordered_1
            if = {
                ordered_in_list = {
                    variable = list_before_order
                    order_by = money_value_rapported_inflation
                    max = 100
                    check_range_bounds = no
                    root = {
                        add_to_variable_list = {
                            name = dependent_economies_list_ordered_1
                            target = prev
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        clear_variable_list = dependent_economies_list
    }
}

          is_reference_type = 1
        }
        root = {
            add_to_variable_list = {

                target = prev
            }
        }
    }
    root  = {
        if = {

                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = list_before_order
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
            }
            clear_variable_list = money_supply_variable_list_ordered_1
            if = {
                ordered_in_list = {
                    variable = list_before_order
                    order_by = total_money_supply
                    max = 10
                    check_range_bounds = no
                    root = {
                        add_to_variable_list = {
                            name = money_supply_variable_list_ordered_1
                            target = prev
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        clear_variable_list = money_supply_variable_list
    }
}
national_capacity_variable_list = {
    every_country = {
        limit = {
            has_modifier = has_central_bank
            NOT = {
                is_subject = yes
                is_subject_type = subject_type_protectorate
            }
        }
        root = {
            add_to_variable_list = {
                name = national_capacity_variable_list
                target = prev
            }
        }
    }
    root  = {
        if = {
            clear_variable_list = list_before_order
            every_in_list = {
                variable = national_capacity_variable_list
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = list_before_order
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
                remove_modifier = global_monetary_reference
            }
            clear_variable_list = national_capacity_variable_list_ordered_1
            ordered_in_list = {
                variable = list_before_order
                order_by = national_capacity
                min = 0
                max = 10
                check_range_bounds = no
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = national_capacity_variable_list_ordered_1
                        target = prev
                    }
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = reference_currency_list_1
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
            }
            clear_variable_list = reference_currency_country_1
            ordered_in_list = {
                variable = reference_currency_list_1
                order_by = national_capacity
                min = 0
                position = 1
                max = 1
                check_range_bounds = no
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = reference_currency_country_1
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
            }
            every_in_list = {
                variable = reference_currency_country_1
                if = {
                    add_modifier = {
                        name = global_monetary_reference
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}
country_index_variable_list = {
    every_country = {
        limit = {
            has_modifier = has_financial_center

                is_subject_type = subject_type_protectorate
            }
        }
        root = {
            add_to_variable_list = {

            }
        }
    }
    root  = {
        if = {
            clear_variable_list = list_before_order
            every_in_list = {
                variable = country_index_variable_list
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = list_before_order
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
                remove_modifier = global_financial_power
            }
            clear_variable_list = country_index_variable_list_ordered_1
            ordered_in_list = {
                variable = list_before_order
                order_by = country_indice
                max = 10
                check_range_bounds = no
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = country_index_variable_list_ordered_1
                        target = prev
                    }
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = financial_power_list_1
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
            }
            clear_variable_list = financial_power_country_1
            ordered_in_list = {
                variable = financial_power_list_1
                order_by = country_indice
                min = 0
                position = 1
                max = 1
                check_range_bounds = no
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = financial_power_country_1
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
            }
            every_in_list = {
                variable = financial_power_country_1
                if = {
                    add_modifier = {
                        name = global_financial_power
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        clear_variable_list = country_index_variable_list
    }

                name = is_subject_list
                target = prev

national_debt_variable_list_clear = {
	root  = {
		clear_variable_list = list_before_order
		every_in_list = {
			variable = central_bank_debt_buyer_list
			root = {
				add_to_variable_list = {
					name = list_before_order
					target = prev
				}
			}
		}
		clear_variable_list = central_bank_debt_buyer_list
		if = {
			ordered_in_list = {
				variable = list_before_order
				order_by = national_debt_compared_gdp
				max = 10
				check_range_bounds = no
				root = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = central_bank_debt_buyer_list
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
central_bank_debt_variable_list = {
    every_country = {
        limit = {
            has_modifier = has_central_bank
			central_bank_debt > 2500000
			#all_gold_owned < 1 
			NOT = {
                is_subject = yes
			}
        }
        root = {
            add_to_variable_list = {
                name = central_bank_debt_variable_list
                target = prev
            }
        }
    }
    root = {
        if = {
            clear_variable_list = list_before_order
            every_in_list = {
                variable = central_bank_debt_variable_list
                root = {
                    add_to_variable_list = {
                        name = list_before_order
                        target = prev
                    }
                }
            }
            clear_global_variable_list = central_bank_debt_variable_list_ordered_1
			ordered_in_list = {
				variable = list_before_order
				order_by = central_bank_debt
				max = 100
				check_range_bounds = no
				root = {
					add_to_global_variable_list = {
						name = central_bank_debt_variable_list_ordered_1
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
        }
        clear_variable_list = central_bank_debt_variable_list
    }


}

#begin_tag_1
	#dinar
	dinar_c_global_stokpile_variable_list = {
	    every_country = {
	        limit = {
	            stockpiling_dinar_state > 0
	        }
	        root = {
	            add_to_variable_list = {
	                name = dinar_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_1
	                target = prev
	            }
	        }
	    }
	    root  = {
	        if = {
	            clear_variable_list = list_before_order
	            every_in_list = {
	                variable = dinar_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_1
	                root = {
	                    add_to_variable_list = {
	                        name = list_before_order
	                        target = prev
	                    }
	                }
	            }
	            clear_variable_list = dinar_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_ordered_1
	            if = {
	                ordered_in_list = {
	                    variable = list_before_order
	                    order_by = stockpiling_dinar_state
	                    max = 10
	                    check_range_bounds = no
	                    root = {
	                        add_to_variable_list = {
	                            name = dinar_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_ordered_1
	                            target = prev
	                        }
	                    }
	                }
	            }
	        }
	        clear_variable_list = money_supply_variable_list
	    }
	}

	        }

	                target = prev
	            }
	        }
	    }
	    root  = {
	        if = {
	            clear_variable_list = list_before_order
	            every_in_list = {
	                variable = gulden_indies_guilder_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_1
	                root = {
	                    add_to_variable_list = {
	                        name = list_before_order
	                        target = prev
	                    }
	                }
	            }
	            clear_variable_list = gulden_indies_guilder_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_ordered_1
	            if = {
	                ordered_in_list = {
	                    variable = list_before_order
	                    order_by = stockpiling_gulden_indies_guilder_state
	                    max = 10
	                    check_range_bounds = no
	                    root = {
	                        add_to_variable_list = {
	                            name = gulden_indies_guilder_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_ordered_1

	#spe_ruble
	spe_ruble_c_global_stokpile_variable_list = {
	    every_country = {
	        limit = {
	            stockpiling_spe_ruble_state > 0
	        }
	        root = {
	            add_to_variable_list = {
	                name = spe_ruble_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_1
	                target = prev
	            }
	        }
	    }
	    root  = {
	        if = {
	            clear_variable_list = list_before_order
	            every_in_list = {
	                variable = spe_ruble_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_1
	                root = {
	                    add_to_variable_list = {
	                        name = list_before_order
	                        target = prev
	                    }
	                }
	            }
	            clear_variable_list = spe_ruble_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_ordered_1
	            if = {
	                ordered_in_list = {
	                    variable = list_before_order
	                    order_by = stockpiling_spe_ruble_state
	                    max = 10
	                    check_range_bounds = no
	                    root = {
	                        add_to_variable_list = {
	                            name = spe_ruble_c_global_stokpile_variable_list_ordered_1
	                            target = prev
	                        }
	                    }
	                }
	            }
	        }
	        clear_variable_list = money_supply_variable_list

#dinar
dinar_currency_law_list = {
	clear_variable_list = dinar_currency_law_list
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = dinar_reference
		}
		remove_modifier = dinar_reference
	}
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_law = law_type:law_dinar_currency
			has_modifier = has_central_bank
		}
		remove_modifier = dinar_reference
		root = {
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = dinar_currency_law_list
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
	root  = {
		if = {
			clear_variable_list = list_before_order
			every_in_list = {
				variable = dinar_currency_law_list
				root = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = list_before_order
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			clear_global_variable_list = dinar_currency_law_list_ordered_1
			if = {
				ordered_in_list = {
					variable = list_before_order
					order_by = national_capacity
					max = 1
					check_range_bounds = no
					root = {
						add_to_global_variable_list = {
							name = dinar_currency_law_list_ordered_1
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_in_global_list = {
				variable = dinar_currency_law_list_ordered_1
				if = {
					remove_modifier = dinar_reference
					add_modifier = {
						name = dinar_reference
					}
					remove_modifier = leading_currency_type
					add_modifier = {
						name = leading_currency_type
					}
				}
			}
		}
		#clear_variable_list = dinar_currency_list
	}
}

#franc_belgian_franc
franc_belgian_franc_currency_law_list = {
	clear_variable_list = franc_belgian_franc_currency_law_list
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = franc_belgian_franc_reference
		}
		remove_modifier = franc_belgian_franc_reference
	}
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_law = law_type:law_franc_belgian_franc_currency
			has_modifier = has_central_bank
		}
		remove_modifier = franc_belgian_franc_reference
		root = {
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = franc_belgian_franc_currency_law_list
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
	root  = {
		if = {
			clear_variable_list = list_before_order
			every_in_list = {
				variable = franc_belgian_franc_currency_law_list
				root = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = list_before_order
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			clear_global_variable_list = franc_belgian_franc_currency_law_list_ordered_1
			if = {
				ordered_in_list = {
					variable = list_before_order
					order_by = national_capacity
					max = 1
					check_range_bounds = no
					root = {
						add_to_global_variable_list = {
							name = franc_belgian_franc_currency_law_list_ordered_1
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_in_global_list = {
				variable = franc_belgian_franc_currency_law_list_ordered_1
				if = {
					remove_modifier = franc_belgian_franc_reference
					add_modifier = {
						name = franc_belgian_franc_reference
					}
					remove_modifier = leading_currency_type
					add_modifier = {
						name = leading_currency_type
					}
				}
			}
		}
		#clear_variable_list = franc_belgian_franc_currency_list
	}
}

			clear_global_variable_list = krone_danish_krone_currency_law_list_ordered_1
			if = {
				ordered_in_list = {
					variable = list_before_order
					order_by = national_capacity
					max = 1
					check_range_bounds = no
					root = {
						add_to_global_variable_list = {
							name = krone_danish_krone_currency_law_list_ordered_1
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_in_global_list = {
				variable = krone_danish_krone_currency_law_list_ordered_1
				if = {
					remove_modifier = krone_danish_krone_reference
					add_modifier = {
						name = krone_danish_krone_reference
					}
					remove_modifier = leading_currency_type
					add_modifier = {
						name = leading_currency_type
					}
				}
			}
		}
		#clear_variable_list = krone_danish_krone_currency_list
	}

		remove_modifier = lira_scudo_sardo_reference
		root = {
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = lira_scudo_sardo_currency_law_list
				target = prev

	}
	root  = {

			every_in_list = {
				variable = lira_scudo_sardo_currency_law_list
				root = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = list_before_order
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			clear_global_variable_list = lira_scudo_sardo_currency_law_list_ordered_1
			if = {
				ordered_in_list = {
					variable = list_before_order
					order_by = national_capacity
					max = 1
					check_range_bounds = no
					root = {
						add_to_global_variable_list = {
							name = lira_scudo_sardo_currency_law_list_ordered_1
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}

			has_law = law_type:law_pound_irish_pound_currency
			has_modifier = has_central_bank
		}
		remove_modifier = pound_irish_pound_reference
		root = {
			add_to_variable_list = {
				name = pound_irish_pound_currency_law_list
				target = prev
			}
		}
	}
	root  = {
		if = {
			clear_variable_list = list_before_order
			every_in_list = {
				variable = pound_irish_pound_currency_law_list
				root = {
					add_to_variable_list = {
						name = list_before_order
						target = prev
					}
				}
			}
			clear_global_variable_list = pound_irish_pound_currency_law_list_ordered_1
			if = {
				ordered_in_list = {
					variable = list_before_order
					order_by = national_capacity
					max = 1
					check_range_bounds = no
					root = {
						add_to_global_variable_list = {
							name = pound_irish_pound_currency_law_list_ordered_1
							target = prev
						}
					}
				}
			}
			every_in_global_list = {
				variable = pound_irish_pound_currency_law_list_ordered_1
				if = {
					remove_modifier = pound_irish_pound_reference
					add_modifier = {
						name = pound_irish_pound_reference
					}
					remove_modifier = leading_currency_type
					add_modifier = {
						name = leading_currency_type
					}
				}
			}
		}
		#clear_variable_list = pound_irish_pound_currency_list
	}
}

	root  = {

						target = prev
					}

					order_by = national_capacity
					max = 1
					check_range_bounds = no
					root = {
						add_to_global_variable_list = {
							name = spe_peseta_currency_law_list_ordered_1
							target = prev
						}
					}
